 Show the flag kejariwal or unke samarthak jab patan ke nikat shankeshwar gaanv pahunche to 10 se 12 graminon ne sadak ke kinare khadey hokar kaale jhande dikhaae
 The villagers shouted slogans against Kejriwal, calling them 'anti-gujarat'
 ek pradarshnkaree ne kaha, 'medha patekar narmada pariyojna ke khilaaf hai
 Narmada is our mother and also the lifeline of Gujarat

 GST (guds and services tex) desh main yadi koi sabase bada tex riform hoga, to isbjatmen yahi ho saktaa he
 This would be the most efficient way of bringing the economy of the entire country into one structure
 na sirf sarkaron ko balki kaarobaariyon, kanjumar or niveshkon ko isse phayda hoga
 The country's economy is expected to increase by 2 percent because of this tax
 yadi arun jetali is bajet main jiesti lagu karne kaa rodmap rakh dete hai, to sambhav he ki iskaa phayda agle vitt varsh se milane lagegaa
 Let's know how -1
 centre or rajya ke apratyaksh kar kaa system ek hi fremawork main aa jayega
 With the introduction of GST, exemption from octroi, central sales tax, state sales tax, entry tax, stamp duty, telecom license fee, turnover tax, tax on transportation of goods and services etc
 will be exempted
 sarkaron ko ek hi tex lagu karnaa hoga or uski vasuuli par dhyaan dena hoga
 2
 kisi bhi utpaada yaa seva kii bikri hone par saplaay chen ke har charan main GST kii vasuuli ek system ke tahat hogi
 Since the last link of the supply chain is the common consumer, it will bear its ultimate weight
 3
 Due to the implementation of only one tax, people will be able to guess the cost of any product or service
 abhi kai tex hone kii vajah se iskaa sahi andaaj nahin lag paata he
 4
 GST ko guds or services par baraabar lagu kiya jayega, jahaan nunatam tex rakhte hue uskaa dayera badhaane kii yojana he
 Which will have the least discount
 taaki tex kaa bhaar zyada bhi na ho or chunki zyada log tex chukaayenge to vasuuli bhi zyada hogi
 5
 visheshgyon kaa maananaa he ki is tex system ke lagu hone se rajya or centre ke bich tex vasuuli kii adchanon or ek bade system ke mentanence se mukti mil jaaegi
 The whole of India will come under the same tax
 6
 It is expected that this system will be more transparent and corruption-free
 7
 Currently, the same product is taxed even when it comes out of the factory and it is taxed even when it is sold at retail outlets
 GST main kisi bhi utpaada par uske upabhokta ke haath main pahunchane par hi tex lagegaa
 As the raw material reaches the factory, the factory will have to pay tax and when the finished product reaches the hands of the consumer, he will have to pay tax
 8
 The country is expected to generate an additional tax income of around Rs 1 lakh crore from the GST
 9
 France first implemented the GST in 1954
 ab 140 deshon main iskaa vajood he
 Brazil and Canada have a dual GST system
 jahaan centre or rajya donon GST vasuul karte hai
 There is also talk of a double GST implementation in India
 taaki rajyon ko apane tex khatm karne ke baad revenue kaa nuksaan na ho
 10
 GST lagu hone se tex pranali aasaan hogi, jisase niryaat ko badhaava milegaa
 Employment is expected to increase
 collegium se tabadale par punarvichaar karne kii maangamdurai bench ke vakeelon ke do sanghathanon ne pradarshan kiyamdras hai court kii chif justise wike tahilarmaani ke tabadale ke virodh main vakil aaj pradarshan kar rahe hai

 madurai bench ke vakeelon ke do sanghathanon ne yah virodh pradarshan kiya or court kii kaarywahi kaa bahishkaar kiya
